# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
Tree ^xaNvfg3k

A tree is a hierarchical data structure consisting of nodes connected by edges. It's a special type of graph with no cycles, meaning there is exactly one path between any two nodes. ^Gm0JFsSJ

Terminology ^RBqUeT1X

Types of Trees ^EqQCcqWS

**Tree Traversal Techniques** ^ESS3gCyF

Binary Tree ^KOFiyrsH

- **Full Binary Tree**: A binary tree where every node has either 0 or 2 children. ^KIpQchHi

- **Complete Binary Tree**: A binary tree in which all levels are fully filled except possibly the last level, which is filled from left to right. ^OAfEQyiP

- **Degenerate (or Pathological) Binary Tree**: A binary tree where each parent node has only one child, resulting in a structure that resembles a linked list. ^eQN06HjV

- **Perfect Binary Tree**: A binary tree where all internal nodes have exactly two children, and all leaf nodes are at the same level. ^8VPiKIV1

- **Balanced Binary Tree**: A binary tree where the height difference between the left and right subtrees for every node is at most one. ^D5zW92n0

Binary Search Tree ^Y6qF7f9n

AVL Tree ^W35rKwbY

Leet Code ^2FVVtEBc

104. Maximum Depth of Binary Tree ^XfblPtAf

100. Same Tree ^RSXZEd0t

226. Invert Binary Tree ^lgrUjxIa

124. Binary Tree Maximum Path Sum ^hrWmSw5W

Given two integer arrays preorder and inorder where preorder is the preorder traversal of a binary tree and inorder is the inorder traversal of the same tree, construct and return the binary tree. ^x1syqJm0

Input: preorder = [3,9,20,15,7], inorder = [9,3,15,20,7] ^tTIn73hz

Output: [3,9,20,null,null,15,7] ^do5bY9PQ

105. Construct Binary Tree from Preorder and Inorder Traversal ^IqUxiT96

Input: root = [1,2,3] ^0wdI3VJJ

Output: 6 ^XhoPFODt

Explanation: The optimal path is 2 -> 1 -> 3 with a path sum of 2 + 1 + 3 = 6. ^UnWFRivt

root = [-10,9,20,null,null,15,7] ^fieJZxzs

Output: 42 ^PPYzoH9I

Explanation: The optimal path is 15 -> 20 -> 7 with a path sum of 15 + 20 + 7 = 42. ^vVZegyvv

    Post Order
BFS ^eMDIF143

IN: 1 2 3
Pre: 2 1 3
Post: 1 3 2  ^du2HCCx7

In Order: 3 5 6 
Pre order: 5 3 6
Post Order: 6 3 5

BFS: 5 3 6 ^YkVHM07x

fun insert(root, val)
    if root is null:
        return Node(val)
    
    if val < root.val:
        root.left = insert(root.left, val)
    else:
        root.right = insert(root.right, val)

    return root ^JgX8wWjg

fun find_min(root):
    current = node
    while current.right
        current = current.left
    return current ^xNvk1LOE

key = 14

fun delete(root, key):

if key < root.val:
    root.left = delete(root.left, key)
else if key > root.val:
    root.right = delete(root.right, key)

else:
    if root.left is None:
        return root.right
    else if root.right is None:
        return root.left

    temp = find_min(root)
    root.val = temp.val
    root.right = delete(root.right, temp.val)

    

 ^YjSKHCGQ
